#  About this item 
  * Stability Upgrade Quick Connection:Supports Bluetooth or WiFi connection.The improved WiFi technology let you quick connection and stay stable,no disconnection worries. Please keep the smart plug connected to your stable 2.4GHz network.(Note: Only 2.4Ghz WiFi) 
  * Hand-Free Voice Control:Smart plugs that work with Alexa and Googel Assistant. Just give a simple voice command to Alexa or Google Assistant to control your connected home devices. Enjoy the joy of smart home devices. 
  * APP Remote Control From Anywhere:You also can control your outlet timers anywhere anytime via the APP directly when you are away. Monitor and control connected electrical equipment in your home.The smart outlet plug compatible with GHome APP, Smart Life App and Tuya App. 
  * Schedules and Timer Function:Easy to set timers and add schedules to connected smart home devices circularly or randomly, making them work as scheduled like auto-off and auto-on to save energy and money. Such as lamps, fan, humidifier, Christmas light timers etc. 
  * Note: To use Alexa and Google Home, please note that this product cannot be connected directly. You need to connect the product to the network and the GHome APP first.

##  Surge Protection 
The built-in surge protector can conduct and divert current in a short period of time to prevent surges from damaging equipment. 
#  User Guide to Start Your Smart Journey 
![GHome Smart Plug,WiFi Smart Plugs](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
  * ### 
Would not connect to Google home？ 
Please try to confirm the network environment and the stability of the device first. 
Tell us the code of the problem product through the Amazon backend. 
Our technical staff and technicians are online 24 hours a day to solve the problem for you. 
  * ### 
Why cannot connect to the Internet?-A 
Make sure that the router has the 2.4G band turned on and connect the device to the network in that band. If the management password is incorrect, check whether the entered number contains special symbols. 
  * ### 
Why cannot connect to the Internet? -B 
Confirm that the router supports the 2.4G frequency band, adjust the AP location away from interference sources (such as operator antennas), and optimize the RF power settings. 
  * ### 
Why cannot connect to the Internet? -C 
The wireless bandwidth of a single wireless router is limited. For example, a common 300M wireless router cannot connect 50 wireless terminals at the same time. In this case, please restart the router. 
  * ### 
Why does the Internet often disconnect? 
Some devices may be taking up too much network resources. You can consider blacklisting them to free up network bandwidth for other devices. In addition, upgrading your router may be an effective solution.

[How customer reviews and ratings work](javascript:void\(0\))
Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.
To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.
[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say
Customers find the smart plug easy to set up, with Alexa walking them through the process with ease, and appreciate its scheduling features and capability to control devices remotely. The connectivity receives mixed feedback - while it works seamlessly with Alexa, some customers find it difficult to connect to smartphones. The functionality and value for money also get mixed reviews, with some saying it works as expected while others report it stops working, and some consider it well worth the price while others find it not worth the investment.

_5 out of 5 stars_
##### Great smart plug
I purchased a 4-pack of these smart plugs for my Christmas lights. One plug worked out of the box, but the others did not. I contacted customer service and had a great experience-Kyle quickly arranged to send a full replacement 4-pack, which arrived very quickly. All of the new plugs worked perfectly. Setup through the app was simple, and the plugs are easy to control, schedule, and automate. After the holidays, I started using them for lamps in my living room and bedrooms, and they’ve worked flawlessly. I haven’t integrated them with Alexa yet, but the setup appears straightforward. The only drawback is the size-they protrude from the outlet and may block another plug on a power strip. Despite that, I highly recommend these smart plugs and would purchase from this company again due to the excellent customer service. I would absolutely buy a slimmer version if one becomes available.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ They Work Well ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R2NR20ABRYPSN4/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)
Reviewed in the United States on January 15, 2026
Number of Items: 2[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
These are in effect a smart switch for your outlets. They work really well to control things like lamps, fans or appliances that can be left "always on" but be controlled by a switched outlet but are a lot more convenient because you can have switched outlets anywhere you put them without having to install a physical switch and run wires or having to install switched outlets. They pair fairly easy. About the only thing that was a little troublesome was getting the GHome app that controls these to work right. I kept getting error 'no network connection' messages so I just uninstalled the app and reinstalled it. I did this once and after that the setup was a breeze. I linked the GHome app to Alexa and Google Home and I control them with both without issue.

#####  Great smart plug 
  
Reviewed in the United States on January 13, 2026 
I purchased a 4-pack of these smart plugs for my Christmas lights. One plug worked out of the box, but the others did not. I contacted customer service and had a great experience-Kyle quickly arranged to send a full replacement 4-pack, which arrived very quickly. All of the new plugs worked perfectly.  
  
Setup through the app was simple, and the plugs are easy to control, schedule, and automate. After the holidays, I started using them for lamps in my living room and bedrooms, and they’ve worked flawlessly. I haven’t integrated them with Alexa yet, but the setup appears straightforward.  
  
The only drawback is the size-they protrude from the outlet and may block another plug on a power strip. Despite that, I highly recommend these smart plugs and would purchase from this company again due to the excellent customer service. I would absolutely buy a slimmer version if one becomes available.

Reviewed in the United States on December 1, 2025
Number of Items: 4[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
These outlets are the best. They are small so you won't kick them as you walk by. I used a flat plug cord with them and the combination sticks out from the wall less than a conventional plug by itself. You can push the button on the outlet to turn them on and off or use the free app to control them remotely. You can set schedules for each one or create a scene. Once you have connected the first one through the app to the wifi, each one after that takes less than 30 seconds to connect and update. Seriously These are the easiest to connect and control. I bought another 4 pack of the round ones and 4 of the dual rectangular ones as well as a dual outdoor one.  
The only drawback is in the app with the pop up ads for other devices. Seriously these are so good and reliable you don't need ads, the brand sells itself.  
  
I will be buying this brand when the need comes up.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Easiest connecting plug ever used! ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R2QWKM8DBE8MSJ/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

These plugs are so far better, setup wise, of any ever used. Previous plugs would require extraneous efforts to try and get connected to my home network or connection would fail as soon as the app was closed. They do use a 2.4 ghz network, which i have a subsetting on my my router for connecting little things, like plugs or devices. I switched my phone to the 2.4 ghz, wireless network, plugged in the device and it displayed "connected" in the Ghome app! I was shocked at the simplicity. Disconnected my phone from that network, rejoined the preferred home wireless, and Alexa announced she found a new plug! Edited the device name (in the app) - the whole process took maybe 2 minutes. I spent probably an hour trying to connect some other plugs (govee) last week and promptly threw them all away. I don't write many reviews, but these are by far the easiest plugs to use and configure and I have tried several. I now have all my plugs on the Ghome app and can see and manage them from the same app instead of multiple apps for management. Easy peezy - get these! Even a non techy person can handle this easily.

## About this Item
  * Stability Upgrade Quick Connection:Supports Bluetooth or WiFi connection.The improved WiFi technology let you quick connection and stay stable,no disconnection worries. Please keep the smart plug connected to your stable 2.4GHz network.(Note: Only 2.4Ghz WiFi)
  * Hand-Free Voice Control:Smart plugs that work with Alexa and Googel Assistant. Just give a simple voice command to Alexa or Google Assistant to control your connected home devices. Enjoy the joy of smart home devices.
  * APP Remote Control From Anywhere:You also can control your outlet timers anywhere anytime via the APP directly when you are away. Monitor and control connected electrical equipment in your home.The smart outlet plug compatible with GHome APP, Smart Life App and Tuya App.
  * Schedules and Timer Function:Easy to set timers and add schedules to connected smart home devices circularly or randomly, making them work as scheduled like auto-off and auto-on to save energy and money. Such as lamps, fan, humidifier, Christmas light timers etc.
  * Note: To use Alexa and Google Home, please note that this product cannot be connected directly. You need to connect the product to the network and the GHome APP first.
